***nicht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nicht.html>nicht</a> (2523)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nichte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nift</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*niftiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nicht.html>nicht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nichten.html>nichten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nichtje.html>nichtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>female cousin; daughter of someone's uncle or aunt</li>
<li>niece; daughter of someone's brother or sister</li>
<li>niece; daughter of someone's brother- or sister-in-law</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sometimes  derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> male homosexual, a gay <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>; in particular one who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> camp or effeminate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achternicht.html>achternicht</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">leernicht</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">nichtendom</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">nichterig</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">relnicht</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">pisnicht</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a> (1429)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The noun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived from Late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:nik.html>nik</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">notch, tally; nock of an arrow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Its further etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unknown; a connection with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">nock</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">notch in a bow to hold the bowstring; notch at the rear of an arrow that fits the bowstring; cleft in the buttocks</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> not <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> clearly established.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p><p>The verb appears to be derived from the noun, though the available evidence <a href = vnd.unilang:shows.html>shows</a> that some of the verb senses predate the noun senses. No connection with <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Germanic languages">Germanic languages</a> such as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">nikke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to nod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nicken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend; to bow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">nikken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to nod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">nicken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>; to sink</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">nicken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend; to depress</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">nicken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to nod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">knicken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend; to <a href = vnd.unilang:snap.html>snap</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">knicken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend; to break</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">hnekka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to nod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">nicka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to nod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> clearly established.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small cut in a surface.
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A particular place or point considered as marked by a <a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a>; the exact point or critical <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">in the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></b> of time</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1603</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michel_de_Montaigne" class="extiw" title="w:Michel de Montaigne"><a href = vnd.unilang:michel.html>Michel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:montaigne.html>Montaigne</a></a>,  “We Taste Nothing Purely”, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Florio" class="extiw" title="w:John Florio">John Florio</a>, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Essays_(Montaigne)" class="extiw" title="w:Essays (Montaigne)">The Essayes,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="or, Morall, Politike and Millitarie Discourses of Lo. Truely he flies when he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> vpon the <b>nicke</b>, and naturally haſtneth to eſcape it, as from [a] ſtep whereon he cannot ſtay or containe himſelfe, and feareth to ſinke into it.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1640</b>,  I. H. [<i>i.e.</i>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Howell" class="extiw" title="w:James Howell">James Howell</a>],  “A Character of Lvrana”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dodona%27s_Grove" class="extiw" title="w:Dodona | s Grove"><span class="polytonic" lang="grc">ΔΕΝΔΡΟΛΟΓΊΑ</span> <span style="font-style: normal;">[</span>DENDROLOGIA<span style="font-style: normal;">]</span>. Mosley [<i>i.e.</i>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphrey_Moseley" class="extiw" title="w:Humphrey Moseley">Humphrey Moseley</a>]<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Princes Arms in St Paules Church-yard.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/987785018">987785018</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=BeRBAQAAMAAJamp;pg=PA62">page 62</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> ſuffred the fatall threed to bee ſpunne out to that length for ſome politique reſpects, and then to cut it off in the very <b>nicke</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1843</b> December 19,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Dickens" class="extiw" title="w:Charles Dickens">Charles Dickens</a>,  “Stave Three. <li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1856</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Browning" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Browning">Robert Browning</a>,  “‘<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Childe_Roland_to_the_Dark_Tower_Came" class="extiw" title="w:Childe Roland to the Dark Tower Came"><a href = vnd.unilang:chillen.html>Childe</a> Roland to the Dark Tower <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>Came</a></a>.’”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Men_and_Women_(poetry_collection)" class="extiw" title="w:Men and Women (poetry collection)"><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>Men</a> and Women</a></cite>, author’s edition, Boston, Mass. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ticknor_and_Fields" class="extiw" title="w:Ticknor and Fields">Ticknor and Fields</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/5857018">5857018</a></small>, stanza 29, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=etcIAAAAQAAJamp;pg=PA104">page 104</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Here ended, then, / Progress this way. When, in the very <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></b> / Of giving up, one time more, <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> a click / As when a <a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a> shuts – you're inside the den!</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A notch cut crosswise in the <a href = vnd.unilang:shank.html>shank</a> of a type, to assist a compositor in placing it properly in the stick, and in distribution.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1841</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Savage_(printer)" class="extiw" title="w:William Savage (printer)">William Savage</a>,  “NICK”, in  <cite>A Dictionary of the Art of Printing</cite>, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Longman" class="extiw" title="w:Longman">Longman, Brown, Green, and Longmans</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/906093397">906093397</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=QLXukDnn4PMCamp;pg=PA543">page 543</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a hollow cast crossways in the <a href = vnd.unilang:shanks.html>shanks</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a>, to make a distinction readily between differnt sorts and sizes; and to enable the compositor to perceive quickly the bottom of the letter as it lies in the case, when composing; as <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b> are always cast on that side of the <a href = vnd.unilang:shank.html>shank</a> on which the bottom of the face of the letter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> placed. A great deal of inconvenience frequently arises, owing to the founders casting different founts of <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a> with a similar <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></b> in each.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1862</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1862_International_Exhibition" class="extiw" title="w:1862 International Exhibition">International Exhibition, 1862</a>. Jurors’ Reports</cite>, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_Bell_%26_Sons" class="extiw" title="w:George Bell amp; Sons">Bell and Daldy</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Fleet Street.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/907777960">907777960</a></small>, class XXVIII, section C (Plate, Letterpress, and Other Modes of Printing), <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=7qk8he-Bvs4Camp;pg=RA16-PA3">page 3</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a> are of the usual thickness and height. In the centre of each type, in the front, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a deep <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></b> of a dovetail shape, which fits upon a metal edge, so that the type cannot be displaced. But of 111 <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a> which are required in the fount, each letter <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> two, three, or four other <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b> cut at right angles, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b> of no one letter being the same as another.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Senses connoting something small.</span>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cricket</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A small deflection of the ball off the edge of the bat, often going to the wicket-keeper for a catch.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  David Fraser,  “The <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a> in White <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Always Right (but He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Not Always Neutral)”, in  <cite>Cricket and the Law: The <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a> in White <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Always Right</cite>, Abingdon, Oxfordshire; New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Routledge" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Routledge">Routledge</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=492RAgAAQBAJamp;pg=PA107">page 107</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Just as a judge may mistakenly believe in the credibility of a clever liar, thereby reaching an 'incorrect decision', an umpire dealing with the blur of a fast bowler and listening for a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></b> of the bat, or lifting his <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> quickly from the bowler's front foot to follow the flight and pitch of the ball to determine if the batter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> out LBW  | <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a> before wicket | , can easily be mistaken.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">genetics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One of the single-stranded <a href = vnd.unilang:dna.html>Dna</a> segments produced during <a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a> translation.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1981</b>,  David Korn |  Paul A. Fisher |  Teresa S.-F. <a href = vnd.unilang:wang.html>Wang</a>,  “Mechanisms of Catalysis of Human <a href = vnd.unilang:dna.html>Dna</a> Polymerases α and β”, in <a href = vnd.unilang:waldo.html>Waldo</a> E. Cohn, editor, <cite>Progress in Nucleic Acid Research and Molecular Biology</cite>, volume 26 (<a href = vnd.unilang:dna.html>Dna</a>: Multiprotein Interactions), New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academic_Press" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Academic Press">Academic Press</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=jWzDdPxj8cECamp;pg=PA66">page 66</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Analysis of the effect of <a href = vnd.unilang:temperaturen.html>temperature</a> on the polymerization reaction with nicked and gapped <a href = vnd.unilang:dna.html>Dna</a> substrates in Mn<small><small style="position:relative;top:-.5em">2+</small></small> (<i>8</i>) [...] reveals identical values of activation energy (<i>E</i><small><sub>a</sub></small>) and <i>Q</i><small><sub>10</sub></small>, indicating that the frequency of productive interactions of polymerase β with 3′-hydroxyl termini at <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b> and gaps <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> indistinguishable and suggesting that localized destabilization of the 5′-terminated <a href = vnd.unilang:dna.html>Dna</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strand.html>strand</a> at the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></b> site does not contribute significantly to the rate-determining step(s) of the synthetic reaction.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2015</b>,  Lesley-Ann Giddings |  David J. Newman,  “Activating the Expression of Natural Product Biosynthetic Gene Clusters”, in  <cite>Bioactive Compounds from Extremophiles: Genomic Studies, Biosynthetic Gene <a href = vnd.unilang:clusters.html>Clusters</a>, and New Dereplication Methods</cite> (SpringerBriefs in Microbiology), <a href = vnd.unilang:cham.html>Cham</a>, Switzerland; Heidelberg |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Springer_Science%2BBusiness_Media" class="extiw" title="w:Springer Science+Business Media">Springer</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Digital_object_identifier" class="extiw" title="w:Digital object identifier">DOI</a>:<span class="neverexpand"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://doi.org/10.1007%2F978-3-319-14836-6">10.1007/978-3-319-14836-6</a></span></small>, <small>→ISBN</small>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Standard_Serial_Number" class="extiw" title="w:International Standard Serial Number">ISSN</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldcat.org/issn/2191-5385">2191-5385</a></small>, section 2.2 (Heterologous Expression), <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=QuoXBgAAQBAJamp;pg=PA13">page 13</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The double-stranded insert and linearized vector are denatured, and the resulting single strands of <a href = vnd.unilang:dna.html>Dna</a> anneal with their overlapping <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a> and extend using each other as a template to form double-stranded circular plasmids with only two <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b>, one on each single <a href = vnd.unilang:strand.html>strand</a>. [...] Lastly, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b> are covalently closed upon transformation into <i>E. coli</i> using its natural repair processes.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2015</b>,  Byong H. <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">in the <a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a> of time</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">nicking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">nicked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To make a <a href="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></a> or notch in; to cut or scratch in a minor way.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">I <b>nicked</b> myself while I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> shaving.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1974</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thea_Astley" class="extiw" title="w:Thea Astley"><a href = vnd.unilang:thea.html>Thea</a> Astley</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Kindness_Cup" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A Kindness Cup">A Kindness Cup</a></cite>, Melbourne, <a href = vnd.unilang:vic.html>Vic</a>. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Nelson_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Nelson (publisher)">Thomas Nelson Australia</a>, <small>→ISBN</small> |  republished Sydney, N.S.W.; Melbourne, <a href = vnd.unilang:vic.html>Vic</a>. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Allen_%26_Unwin" class="extiw" title="w:Allen amp; Unwin"><a href = vnd.unilang:allen.html>Allen</a> amp; Unwin House of Books</a>, 2012, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=sDKllVxqJ7oCamp;pg=PA1">pages 1–2</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">This <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> pauses in his shaving to squint at the piece of paper again, razor hesitant, eye returning anxious but reluctant to the blurred <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a>. [...] He <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b> himself and the tired blood trickles a <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:stops.html>stops</a> easily these days almost before the cotton-wool <a href = vnd.unilang:sticks.html>sticks</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">nicker</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">nicking</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">noun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a>(name)</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Internet</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Clipping of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">nickname</i></span></span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">a user’s reserved <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></b> on an IRC network</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1995</b>,  Donald <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>Rose</a>,  <cite>Internet Chat Quick Tour: Real-time Conversations amp; Communications Online</cite>, Chapel Hill, N.C. |  <a href = vnd.unilang:ventana.html>Ventana</a> Press, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 42:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><i>/<a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a> lt;new-nicknamegt;</i> Changes your nickname—the name by which other IRCers see and refer to you—to anything you'd like (but remember that nine characters <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the maximum <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></b> length).</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:josh.html>Josh</a> Datko,  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=i2OZBAAAQBAJamp;pg=PT204">Chatting Off-the-record</a>”, in  <cite>BeagleBone for Secret Agents: Bbrowse Anonymously, Communicate Secretly, and Create Custom Security Solutions with Open Source Software, the BeagleBone Black, and Cryptographic Hardware</cite> (Community Experience Distilled), Birmingham, West Midlands |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Packt" class="extiw" title="w:Packt">Packt Publishing</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Also, ERC, like Emacs, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> extremely modular and flexible. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, of course, a free software program, but there are also many existing <a href = vnd.unilang:modules.html>modules</a> from <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></b> highlighting to autoaway that you can use.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">nicking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">nicked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To give or call (someone) by a nickname; to style.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1634</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Ford_(dramatist)" class="extiw" title="w:John Ford (dramatist)">[John Ford]</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Perkin_Warbeck_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:Perkin Warbeck (play)">The Chronicle <a href = vnd.unilang:historie.html>Historie</a> of Perkin Warbeck. A Strange Truth.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Acted (some-times) by the Queenes Maiestie’s Servants at the Phenix in Drurie Lane.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Purfoot" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Purfoot"><a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>[homas] P[urfoot, Jr.]</a> for Hugh Beeston,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="and are to be sold at his shop, neere the Castle in Corne-hill.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/81300826">81300826</a></small> |  republished as  <cite>A Chronicle History of Perkin Warbeck. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nix.html>nix</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">nixie</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:nix.html>nix</a> or <span class="Latn" lang="en">nixie</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">water spirit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1879</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Viktor_Rydberg" class="extiw" title="w:Viktor Rydberg"><a href = vnd.unilang:viktor.html>Viktor</a> Rydberg</a>,  “The Magic of the People and the Struggle of the Church against It”, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/August_Hjalmar_Edgren" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:August Hjalmar Edgren">August Hjalmar Edgren</a>, transl., <cite>The Magic of the Middle Ages: <a href = vnd.unilang:translated.html>Translated</a> from the Swedish</cite>, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Holt_and_Company" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry Holt and Company"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Holt and Company</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/3814209">3814209</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/magicofmiddleag00rydb/page/201/mode/1up">page 201</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">[A]midst <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ahriman" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ahriman">Ahriman</a> and his hosts who <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> now established themselves in the Occident, and as heirs to the horns and <a href = vnd.unilang:tails.html>tails</a> of Pans and fauns, a crowd of native <a href = vnd.unilang:spirits.html>spirits</a> moved; imps, giants, trolls, forest-spirits, elves and hobgoblins in and on the earth; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nicks.html>nicks</a></b>, river-sprites in the water, fiends in the air, and <a href = vnd.unilang:salamanders.html>salamanders</a> in the fire.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>While the spelling <i><a href = vnd.unilang:nie.html>nie</a></i> and the <u>invariable</u> use of the corresponding pronunciation are dialectal, the standard word <i><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not rarely given the same pronunciation, particularly in fast speech.</li></ul>

***nier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nier.html>nier</a> (9415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">niere</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*neurô</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*negʷʰrós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A kidney.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">especially in the diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An animal kidney eaten as a food.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aten.html>aten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pastei.html>pastei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:niertjes.html>niertjes</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>ate</a> a pasty with <b>kidneys</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***niet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> (8)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">niwet</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*niowiht</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">niewiht</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">nio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">never</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wiht</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing, creature</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The former in turn derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ne</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiw-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ever</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wiht-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> originally a pronoun meaning "not a thing", and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> used to reinforce a regular negation. The pronomial meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> in Middle Dutch. English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">not</i>, and its older forms <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">naught</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">nought</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> formed in the same way, but "not" also <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> its sense as a pronoun and became a negation adverb as in Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>Not, no: <span class="use-with-mention">used to express negation.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>Niet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:storen.html>storen</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do <b>not</b> disturb!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>not</b> true.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieten.html>nieten</a> (68503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to staple
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naaimachine.html>naaimachine</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naait.html>naait</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nietmachine.html>nietmachine</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A sewing machine sews and a stapler <b>staples</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***niezen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:niezen.html>niezen</a> (15274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:niesen.html>niesen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*niesan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hneusaną</i>. Because of the onomatopoeic character of the word, variant forms with different initial consonants also exist(ed), such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">fniezen</i> (from Proto-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fneusaną</i>) and English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sneeze</i>.
</p>

***nightingale.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a> (29775)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">nyghtyngale</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">niȝtingale</i>, alteration (with intrusive <i>n</i>) of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">nyghtgale</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">nightegale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">nihtegala</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">nihtegale</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a>; night-raven</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">night-singer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nahtigalǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">night</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gale</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Noachtegoal</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nachtegaal.html>nachtegaal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Nachtigall</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Nachtigall</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">nattergal</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></span><span title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">næturgali</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">nightingales</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A European songbird, <i>Luscinia megarhynchos</i>, of the family Muscicapidae.
<ul><li><b>1826</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mary_Shelley" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mary Shelley"><a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Shelley</a>, chapter 5 in the first part of <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Last_Man" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Last Man">The Last <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a></a></i>
<dl><dd>The oaks around <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> the home of a tribe of <b>nightingales</b></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>Nightingales</b> have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> spotted in this coppice.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">You sing like a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></b>, sport!</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">philomel</span></li></ul>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Named after <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florence_Nightingale" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Florence Nightingale">Florence <a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>Nightingale</a></a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">nightingales</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of flannel scarf with sleeves, formerly worn by invalids when sitting up in <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>.</li></ol>

***nihilisme.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nihilisme.html>nihilisme</a> (74065)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Nihilismus</i>, itself from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:nihil.html>nihil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nil, nothing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + German -ismus '-ism', coined in 1817 by German philosopher Friedrich Heinrich Jacobi, but repeatedly 'reinvented'.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nihilisme.html>nihilisme</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nihilisme.html>nihilismes</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nihilisme.html>nihilismes</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nihilisme.html>nihilismethe</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">nihilism</span></li>
<li>(<i>also capitalized: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nihilisme.html>Nihilisme</a></b></i>) <span class="Latn" lang="en">Nihilism</span></li></ol>

***nijlpaard.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nijlpaard.html>nijlpaard</a> (16800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Nijl</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Nile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paard.html>paard</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a loose calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hippopotamus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἱπποπόταμος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hippopótamos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The same in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Nilpferd</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nijlpaard.html>nijlpaard</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nijlpaarden.html>nijlpaarden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nijlpaard.html>nijlpaardje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">hippopotamus</span>, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Hippopotamus_amphibius" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Hippopotamus amphibius"><i>Hippopotamus amphibius</i></a></span>
<ul><li><b>2016</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:anke.html>Anke</a> Kranendonk, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nijlpaard.html>nijlpaard</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:juf.html>juf</a></i>, Zwijsen <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeverij.html>Uitgeverij</a>, →ISBN.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">‘Hemeltjelief,’ <a href = vnd.unilang:zegt.html>zegt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:juf.html>juf</a> Lieke. ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nijlpaard.html>nijlpaard</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jullie.html>jullie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dak.html>dak</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afschuwelijke.html>afschuwelijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebeurtenis.html>gebeurtenis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijkt.html>lijkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertel.html>vertel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geblesseerd.html>geblesseerd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geraakt.html>geraakt</a>, of <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plat.html>plat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dubbeltje.html>dubbeltje</a>?’</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">"Heavens to Betsy," says Ms Lieke (teacher). "A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hippo.html>hippo</a></b> on your (pl.) roof? That <a href = vnd.unilang:sounds.html>sounds</a> like a horrible thing to happen to you. Tell <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> somebody get injured or get as <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> as a pancake?"</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">hippopotamus</span>, any of the Hippopotamidae
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">rivierpaard</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***nikker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nikker.html>nikker</a> (3619)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nicker</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nix.html>nix</a>, nixie</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nikwus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nix.html>nix</a>, water-sprite</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nikker.html>nikker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nikkers.html>nikkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nikker.html>nikkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A water spirit, especially one who lures (young) people to drown; a neck, <a href = vnd.unilang:nix.html>nix</a>, nixie
<ul><li><b>1873</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. Rijkens, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reiziger.html>reiziger</a>. Aardrijkskundige <a href = vnd.unilang:beschrijvingen.html>beschrijvingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schilderingen.html>schilderingen</a>. Leesboek <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoogste.html>hoogste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klasse.html>klasse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> lagereschool</i>, J. B. Wolters (3rd revised ed.), page 94.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:volk.html>volk</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nabijheid.html>nabijheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> hooge bergmeren <a href = vnd.unilang:gelooft.html>gelooft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:allerlei.html>allerlei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kobolden.html>kobolden</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:elfen.html>elfen</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nikkers.html>nikkers</a></b>, water- <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> berggeesten.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nix.html>nix</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:watergeest.html>watergeest</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">nigger</i>, but also influenced by etymology 1 as nixies <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> believed to be of a dark colour.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nikker.html>nikker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nikkers.html>nikkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nikker.html>nikkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ethnic slur</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A nigger</li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> beledigende term <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:neger.html>neger</a>", <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorspronkelijk.html>oorspronkelijke</a> donkerhuidige <a href = vnd.unilang:bewoner.html>bewoner</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afrika.html>Afrika</a> ten <a href = vnd.unilang:zuiden.html>zuiden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Sahara</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:niks.html>niks</a> (152)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from colloquial and dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:nix.html>nix</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niks.html>niks</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>nothing</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niks.html>niks</a></strong> (<i>used only predicatively</i>, <i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niks.html>niks</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niks.html>niks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>disagreeable, distasteful, not liking
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vind.html>vind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:niks.html>niks</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huizen.html>huizen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bouwen.html>bouwen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> like</b> that they're going to build <a href = vnd.unilang:houses.html>houses</a> here.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>uninteresting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>Jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schilderijen.html>schilderijen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geweldig.html>geweldig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:niks.html>niks</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You may think these paintings are great, but they're <b>not interesting</b> for <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niks.html>niks</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nothing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">use</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Nichtsnutz</i>.

***nim.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nim.html>nim</a> (9715)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">nimen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">niman</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nemaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*nem-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to give or take one's due</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">nieme</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">nimme</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">nehmen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">nehmen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">nemme</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to learn, grasp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">numb</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">nimble</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nim.html>nim</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">nims</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">nimming</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">nimmed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To take or seize.
<ul><li><b>1381</b>, <i>Pegge Cook. Recipes</i>, page 114, quoted in <b>1962</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hans_Kurath" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Hans Kurath"><a href = vnd.unilang:hans.html>Hans</a> Kurath</a> amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:sherman.html>Sherman</a> M. Kuhn, eds., <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English_Dictionary" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Middle English Dictionary">Middle English Dictionary</a></i>, Ann Arbor, <a href = vnd.unilang:mich.html>Mich</a>.: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Michigan_Press" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:University of Michigan Press">University of Michigan Press</a>, ISBN 978-0-472-01044-8, page 1242, in the entry "dorrẹ̄, dōrī adj. amp; n. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <u>cook</u>":
<dl><dd>For to make Soupys dorry. <b>Nym</b> onyons <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <b>Nym</b> wyn <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> toste wyte bred and do yt in dischis, and <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a> Almande mylk.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1547</b> (original; printed <b>1870</b>), Andrew <a href = vnd.unilang:boorde.html>Boorde</a>, <i>The First <a href = vnd.unilang:bo.html>Boke</a> of the Introduction of Knowledge</i>, page 122:
<dl><dd>Ich <a href = vnd.unilang:cham.html>cham</a> a Cornysche <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a>[e] <a href = vnd.unilang:che.html>che</a> can brew; [...] <b>Nym</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> a quart of <a href = vnd.unilang:ale.html>ale</a>, that iche may it of sup.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1566–1573</b> (original; printed <b>1873</b>), John Partridge, <i>The Hystorie of the Moste Noble Knight Plasidas, and Other <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>Rare</a> Pieces</i>, page 106:
<dl><dd>Then Alfyne to the court Of Syleuma doth come, / And Pandauola in her armes / Her Alfyne hath up <b>num</b> / And kisseth him full <a href = vnd.unilang:ofte.html>ofte</a> <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2017</b>, Thomas Heywood, <i>A Woman Killed With Kindness</i>, Bloomsbury Publishing (→ISBN), page 155:
<dl><dd>Gryndall carefully <a href = vnd.unilang:sets.html>sets</a> out the difference between seizing or <b>nimming</b> a bird (an outcome that would constitute a partly successful flight) and taking the bird outright:  | And if your <a href = vnd.unilang:hawke.html>Hawke</a> noume [<a href = vnd.unilang:nim.html>nim</a>, seize] a foule, and the foule breake from her, she hath discomfited many <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a> of the foule, and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> broken away: but in kindly speech you shall say, your <a href = vnd.unilang:hawke.html>hawke</a> hath noumed or seased a foule, and not <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> it'.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To filch, steal.
<ul><li><b>1663</b>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hudibras" class="extiw" title="w:Hudibras">Hudibras</a></i>, by Samuel <a href = vnd.unilang:butler.html>Butler</a>, part 1, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Hudibras/Part_1/Canto_1" class="extiw" title="s:Hudibras/Part 1/Canto 1">canto 1</a>
<dl><dd>They'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> question <a href = vnd.unilang:mars.html>Mars</a>, and, by his look, \ Detect who 'twas that <b>nimm'd</b> a cloak;</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1785</b>, Hutton, <i>Bran New Wark</i>, I. 305, quoted in <b>1903</b>, Joseph Wright, <i>The English Dialect Dictionary: M-Q</i>, page 273:
<dl><dd><b>Nimming</b> and niftering whativver he can try his fists on.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1821</b>, Apuleius, <i>The Golden Ass of <a href = vnd.unilang:lucius.html>Lucius</a> Apuleius, of Medaura</i>, page 131:
<dl><dd>But while he fell in some <a href = vnd.unilang:brave.html>brave</a> exploit, you, I suppose, being provident rogues and <a href = vnd.unilang:thieves.html>thieves</a> of discretion, <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> on the sure lay, pilfering little thefts among the mob, fearfully <b>nimming</b> a cloak or rifling some old woman's bulk of a stock to set up a piece-broker's shop.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1824</b> (edition; original 1790), Nairne, <i>Tales</i>, 37, quoted in <b>1903</b>, Joseph Wright, <i>The English Dialect Dictionary: M-Q</i>, page 273:
<dl><dd>They <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nim.html>nim</a></b> a pig, a duck, or fowl.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1854</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a> Oldham, <i>Oldham's Amusing and Instructive Reader: A Course of Reading, Original and Selected, in Prose and Poetry, Wherein <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>Wit</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:humor.html>Humor</a>, and Mirth are Made the Means of Awakening Interest, and Imparting Instructon : for the Use of Schools and <a href = vnd.unilang:academies.html>Academies</a></i>, page 110:
<dl><dd>Shall <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> go <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:nim.html>nim</a></b></i> a horse, <a href = vnd.unilang:tom.html>Tom</a>,—what dost think? [...] <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:nim.html>Nim</a></b></i>? yes, yes, yes, let | s <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nim.html>nim</a></b> with all my heart; I see no harm in <i><b>nimming</b></i>, for my part; [...] <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>Were</a> it my lord mayor's Hourse—I'd <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nim.html>nim</a></b> it first. [...A horse] they stole, or, as they called it, <i><b>nimmed</b></i>, / Just as the twilight all the landscape dimmed. [...] What <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> most likely, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that both these elves / <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>Were</a>, in like manner, halter-<b>nimmed</b> themselves.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To walk with short, quick strides; trip along.
<ul><li><b>1856</b>, Thompson, <i>Hist. Boston</i>, page 716, quoted in <b>1903</b>, Joseph Wright, <i>The English Dialect Dictionary: M-Q</i>, page 273:
<dl><dd>The old lady does <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nim.html>nim</a></b> along.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1949</b>, Wilfrid J. <a href = vnd.unilang:halliday.html>Halliday</a>, Arthur Stanley Umpleby, <i>The White <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>Rose</a> Garland of Yorkshire Dialect Verse and Local and Folk-lore Rhymes</i>, quoting <a href = vnd.unilang:irene.html>Irene</a> Sutcliffe, page 111:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>Ah</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> set myself doon where the aums meet aboon, / When Jinny jamp oop, and ganned <b>nimming</b> alang.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
