</p>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nim" class="extiw" title="w:nim"><a href = vnd.unilang:nim.html>nim</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nim" class="extiw" title="w:nim">Wikipedia </a></span></div>

***nimbus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nimbus.html>nimbus</a> (74062)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:nimbus.html>nimbus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dark cloud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nimbus.html>nimbus</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">nimbi</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">nimbuses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A circle of light; a halo.</li>
<li>A gray rain cloud.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">circle of light</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> In heraldry and art, a <a href = vnd.unilang:nimbus.html>nimbus</a> may be considered distinct from a halo. The term <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">halo</i> can refer to an open <a href = vnd.unilang:ring.html>ring</a> of light or of gold behind the head of a saint, while <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nimbus.html>nimbus</a></i> refers to a solid disk of light or gold.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">circle of light</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">halo</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">nimbed</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:nimbus.html>nimbus</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ring.html>ring</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aureool.html>aureool</a>, heiligenkrans, stralenkrans, halo</li>

***nimf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nimf.html>nimf</a> (44990)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nymphe</i>. Borrowed from Old or Middle French, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">nympha</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νύμφη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">númphē</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Greek mythology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Roman mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">nymph</span>, female lesser divinity of nature</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">entomology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">nymph</span>, juvenile form of a hemimetabolous insect</li></ol>

***nit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nit.html>nit</a> (102416)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">nite</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hnitu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hnits</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neet.html>neet</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Nisse</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no"><a href = vnd.unilang:nit.html>nit</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱ(<a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>)nid-</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scottish_Gaelic" class="extiw" title="w:Scottish Gaelic">Scottish Gaelic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gd">sneadh</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">glìnda</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">gnida</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">thëri</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κονίς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konís</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nit.html>nit</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">nits</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The egg of a louse.</li>
<li>A young louse.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ireland" class="extiw" title="w:Ireland">Ireland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A head louse regardless of its age.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fool, a <a href = vnd.unilang:nitwit.html>nitwit</a>.</li>
<li>A nitpicker.</li>
<li>A minor shortcoming.</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nix.html>nix</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">nixie</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">water spirit</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>1956</b>, <i>S-Gravenhage. <a href = vnd.unilang:maandblad.html>Maandblad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemeente.html>gemeente</a> 'S-Gravenhage</i>, page 14.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nix.html>nixen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Heinrich <a href = vnd.unilang:heine.html>Heine</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zwanen.html>zwanen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Scandinavische <a href = vnd.unilang:ballades.html>ballades</a>?</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Are these then Heinrich <a href = vnd.unilang:heine.html>Heine</a>'s <b>nixes</b> or the <a href = vnd.unilang:swans.html>swans</a> of Scandinavian ballads?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nikker.html>nikker</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:watergeest.html>watergeest</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:nuh.html>nuh</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">still</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nodig.html>nodig</a> (131)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*naudigaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">needy</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">nötig</i>); synchronically analyzable as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nood.html>nood</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nodig.html>nodig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nodig.html>nodiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">nodigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>necessary, needed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nodig.html>nodig</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That's not <b>necessary</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only in attribute position</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> some amount or degree of, a certain level of, some</li></ol>

***noemen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:noemen.html>noemen</a> (604)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:noemen.html>noemen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nuomen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nōmijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:noemen.html>noemen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to call, to name</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mention</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> proscribed<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have as one's name
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:noemt.html>noemt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What's your name?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The sense “to have as name” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> proscribed and limited to parts of Belgium. The standard verb for this sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heten.html>heten</a></i>.
</p>
